## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="64e5c-1610">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="64e5c-1610">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="64e5c-1611">A classe **MS-DFSR-Member** faz parte do suporte ao serviço de replicação do sistema de arquivos distribuído (DFS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="64e5c-1611">The **ms-DFSR-Member** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
